Motivation: LLM直接作为诊断引擎存在对提示词敏感、输出不稳定等问题，而传统结构化ML模型需要表格输入难以融入临床叙事工作流，需要一种兼具自然语言处理能力和稳定预测性能的混合方法。

Method: ClaMPAPP使用LLM从叙事文本中提取符合模式约束的临床特征，经过确定性合理性检查后，将验证后的特征输入XGBoost分类器进行预测；通过模板渲染和约束LLM重写生成测试数据，并设计句子顺序排列实验评估位置鲁棒性。

Result: ClaMPAPP在内部和外部验证中均取得最优诊断性能，漏诊阑尾炎病例最少；端到端LLM的敏感度-特异度平衡不稳定，且在叙事重排序下性能退化更严重。

Conclusion: LLM作为接口、ML作为预测器的分离设计既能提供自然语言可用性，又能保证稳定的预测性能，为临床决策支持提供了更可审计的技术路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can make clinical decision support more accessible by interpreting free-text documentation, but their direct use as diagnostic engines is limited by sensitivity to prompts, information order, and plausible but incorrect outputs. Structured machine-learning models offer more stable risk prediction, yet they require tabular inputs that are difficult to integrate with narrative clinical workflows. We present ClaMPAPP (Clinical Language-assisted Machine-learning Pipeline for Appendicitis), a hybrid system that uses an LLM as an interface rather than as the final decision-maker. ClaMPAPP extracts schema-constrained clinical features from note-like narratives, applies deterministic plausibility checks, and passes validated features to an XGBoost classifier trained on clinical, laboratory, and ultrasound variables. We evaluated ClaMPAPP on two independent pediatric appendicitis cohorts from German hospitals and compared it with end-to-end LLM baselines, including open-source and proprietary models. To preserve ground truth while testing free-text input, narratives were generated from structured electronic health records through template rendering and constrained LLM rewriting, with additional sentence-order permutation to assess positional robustness. ClaMPAPP achieved the strongest overall diagnostic performance in both internal and external validation while minimizing missed appendicitis cases, the key safety concern in acute triage. End-to-end LLMs showed unstable sensitivity-specificity trade-offs and greater degradation under narrative reordering. These results support an LLM-as-interface, ML-as-predictor design that separates natural-language usability from predictive inference and provides a more auditable pathway for clinical decision support.

</details>


### [136] [RECOM: A Validity Discrimination Tradeoff in Automatic Metrics for Open Ended Reddit Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19218)
*Pushwitha Krishnappa,Amit Das,Vinija Jain,Aman Chadha,Tathagata Mukherjee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 现有自动评估指标在开放型问答中无法同时保证有效性和区分力，存在内在权衡；本文发布RECOM数据集并系统验证了这一矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动评估指标被默认用于两个任务：衡量生成内容与真实内容的对齐程度（有效性），以及区分不同系统的优劣（区分力）。在开放型、观点驱动的问答中，这两个任务存在冲突，但此前未被系统研究。

Method: 构建RECOM数据集（15,000条Reddit问答，数据截止于所有模型训练之后，避免污染）；对5个开源LLM（7-10B）的输出，使用多种指标（余弦相似度、BERTScore等）评分，并引入随机排列噪声基线进行对比分析。

Result: 余弦相似度能有效区分真实回复与随机回复（Cohen's d≈2），但无法区分不同模型（|d|<0.1）；BERTScore precision看似能区分模型（|d|达0.63），但控制响应长度后降至|d|=0.09，且有效性弱（d≈0.8）。三名独立LLM评委同样重现了有效性与区分力之间的差距。

Conclusion: 有效性与区分力之间的权衡是评估指标本身的设计问题，而非模型差异所致，源于表示设计。建议在双轴上报告指标，并明确加入随机基线。RECOM数据集已公开。

Abstract: Automatic metrics are the default for evaluating LLM-generated text, yet a metric is quietly asked to do two jobs: tell genuine content alignment from surface coincidence (validity), and tell a better system from a worse one (discriminative power). On open-ended, opinion-driven question answering, the two are in tension. We introduce RECOM (Reddit Evaluation for Correspondence of Models), a contamination-free evaluation dataset of 15,000 r/AskReddit questions (September 2025), each paired with its authentic community replies, which postdate every evaluated model's training cutoff. Scoring five open-source LLMs (7--10B) against every reply each metric paired with a random-derangement noise floor we find that no metric does both jobs well. Cosine similarity separates real from random answers (Cohen's $d \approx 2$) but cannot rank the five models ($|d| < 0.1$); BERTScore precision appears to rank the models (raw $|d|$ up to 0.63), but once response length is controlled this collapses to $|d| = 0.09$ and its validity is weak ($d \approx 0.8$, versus cosine's $\approx 2$). Because every metric scores the same outputs, this validity--discrimination tradeoff is a property of the metrics, not the models, and we argue it stems from representation design. Three independent LLM judges reproduce the validity gap and likewise separate the five models only weakly. We recommend reporting metrics on both axes, with an explicit random-baseline floor. RECOM is publicly available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/recom-D4B0

</details>


### [137] [DreamReasoner-8B: Block-Size Curriculum Learning for Diffusion Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19257)
*Zirui Wu,Lin Zheng,Jiacheng Ye,Shansan Gong,Xueliang Zhao,Yansong Feng,Wei Bi,Lingpeng Kong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出DreamReasoner-8B，一个基于块扩散的推理模型。研究发现大块训练导致推理性能差，小块训练则有效。为此提出块大小课程学习（从细粒度到粗粒度过渡），解决了粒度差距。在数学和代码推理基准上达到与Qwen3-8B等领先自回归模型竞争的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索块扩散语言模型能否可靠地扩展到长链式推理（CoT）任务，解决训练与推理时块大小对推理性能的影响问题。

Method: 1) 开发DreamReasoner-8B开源块扩散推理模型；2) 系统研究训练和推理块大小对长CoT推理的影响；3) 提出块大小课程学习，从细粒度到粗粒度逐步过渡训练。

Result: 大块训练导致推理性能极差，小块训练保留有效推理；块大小课程学习克服了粒度差距，使模型在不同推理块大小下均表现良好；DreamReasoner-8B在数学和代码推理任务上与Qwen3-8B等模型性能相当。

Conclusion: 块扩散模型通过课程学习可以有效扩展至长CoT推理任务，为高效、具备推理能力的扩散语言模型奠定了实践基础。

Abstract: Block diffusion language models accelerate decoding through parallel block-wise denoising, yet whether they can be reliably scaled for long chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning remains unresolved. To this end, we develop DreamReasoner-8B, an open-source block diffusion reasoning model, and conduct a systematic study of how training and inference block sizes affect long-CoT reasoning. Our analysis reveals a stark performance disparity: training with large block sizes yields remarkably poor reasoning, whereas small block sizes preserve effective reasoning. To bridge this granularity gap, we propose block-size curriculum learning, which gradually transitions training from fine-grained to coarse-grained block sizes, thereby overcoming this limitation and enabling strong reasoning performance that generalizes across diverse inference block sizes. On mathematical and code reasoning benchmarks, DreamReasoner-8B achieves results competitive with leading open autoregressive models such as Qwen3-8B. This work establishes a practical foundation for efficient, reasoning-capable diffusion language models. We release our model at https://github.com/DreamLM/DreamReasoner.

</details>


### [138] [Trade-offs in Medical LLM Adaptation: An Empirical Study in French QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19266)
*Ikram Belmadani,Oumaima El Khettari,Carlos Ramisch,Frederic Bechet,Richard Dufour,Benoit Favre*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了持续预训练(CPT)、监督微调(SFT)及其组合在法语医学问答领域的适应效果，发现SFT在多项选择问答中性价比最高，而CPT在开放式问答中能提升指标但SFT可能降低生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型(LLM)在专业领域和语言的适应策略效果尚不明确，需要进行系统性研究来厘清不同适应策略的优劣。

Method: 以法语医学问答为案例，比较CPT、SFT及两者组合三种适应策略，跨三个模型家族、多种规模和三种初始化类型，分别评估多项选择和开放式问答，使用自动指标和LLM-as-a-Judge评估。

Result: 多项选择问答中CPT+SFT效果最好但提升不显著；开放式问答中CPT提升重叠指标，SFT常降低生成质量；指令微调和CPT+SFT在LLM评估中更受青睐；法语适应可有效迁移到英语任务。

Conclusion: 提供了在计算资源约束下选择适应策略的实用指南，SFT是多项选择问答的强基线，而开放问答需根据评估指标选择策略。

Abstract: The development of large language models (LLMs) has led to an increased focus on their adaptation to specialized domains and languages, yet the effectiveness of domain adaptation strategies remains unclear. We present a study of medical domain adaptation using French medical question-answering (QA) as a case study. We compare continual pretraining (CPT), supervised fine-tuning (SFT), and their combination across three model families, multiple sizes, and three initialization types, explicitly disentangling adaptation effects from base model choice. We evaluate both multiple-choice (MCQA) and open-ended QA (OEQA) under greedy and constrained decoding using automatic metrics and LLM-as-a-Judge evaluation. For MCQA, CPT+SFT most often achieves the best scores, but gains over SFT are small and frequently not statistically significant, making SFT a strong and cost-effective default. For OEQA, CPT consistently improves overlap-based metrics, while SFT often degrades generation quality; instruction tuning and CPT+SFT are preferred by LLM-based evaluation. Cross-lingual experiments further show effective transfer from French adaptation to English benchmarks. Overall, we provide practical guidelines for selecting adaptation strategies under computational constraints.

### [139] [Enhancing Decision-Making with Large Language Models through Multi-Agent Fictitious Play](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19308)
*Leyang Shen,Yang Zhang,Xiaoyan Zhao,Chun Kai Ling,Tat-Seng Chua*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出多智能体虚构博弈（MAFP）框架，通过博弈论中的虚构博弈原理，解决LLM多智能体系统中因立场纠缠而导致的决策复杂性问题，在竞争性决策任务中优于现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体系统擅长分解执行复杂任务，但无法处理需要多方利益相关者同时推理且决策相互依赖的决策任务，即“立场纠缠”问题。

Method: 提出多智能体虚构博弈（MAFP），将利益相关者立场建模为智能体，通过迭代地让每个智能体对其他智能体历史决策的经验混合做出最佳响应，逼近博弈均衡。

Result: 在竞争性决策任务中，MAFP在锦标赛强度和鲁棒性两个互补指标上均优于单轮和多轮基线方法。

Conclusion: MAFP能有效应对立场纠缠问题，通过暴露和解决彼此的弱点，逐步提升决策质量和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent systems (MAS) have demonstrated great potential in solving tasks with execution complexity, by distributing subtasks across cooperative agents. However, this divide-and-conquer paradigm falls short on decision-making tasks that are also prevalent in the real world. These tasks require simultaneous reasoning from the stances of all involved stakeholders whose decisions are mutually dependent and thus cannot be solved in isolation. We characterize this challenge as stance entanglement, a form of decision complexity distinct from execution complexity. To address it, we propose Multi-Agent Fictitious Play (MAFP), a novel MAS paradigm that represents stakeholder stances as agents and formulates decision-making as an equilibrium-seeking process. Built on the game-theoretic principle of fictitious play, MAFP iteratively updates each agent's decision by best responding to the empirical mixture of other agents' past decisions. This enables agents to expose and address one another's weaknesses, progressively improving decision quality and robustness. We evaluate MAFP on challenging decision-making tasks that test the capability of deciding strategies for competitive scenarios prior to acting. MAFP outperforms both single-round and multi-round baselines on two complementary metrics, tournament strength and robustness, demonstrating its effectiveness in addressing stance entanglement.

</details>

*Denis Peskoff,Joe Barrow,Christopher Vu,Diag Davenport*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 美国地方条例（县市法规）是日常监管的重要法律层级，但目前分散在不同供应商平台上，仅支持人工浏览而非批量机器读取，严重制约了法律AI的发展。

Method: 1) 构建包含9,239个市县条例的原始语料库；2) 创建覆盖2,309个县（美国3,144个县中最大）的县级统一访问层；3) 使用OCR处理多种文档格式；4) 训练基于ModernBERT的分类器和评分器，用于分析地方法律的多个维度（如模糊性和家长主义）。

Result: 原始语料包含9,239个市县条例；县级访问层覆盖2,309个县（占美国县总数的73.4%），覆盖大多数美国人口；提供了覆盖元数据以支持可复现性。

Conclusion: LOCUS填补了美国法律AI中地方条例数据缺失的关键空白，为法律AI研究提供了机器可读的地方法律资源，支持未来扩展和下游研究。

Abstract: Progress in legal AI increasingly depends on access to authoritative legal text at scale. Yet one of the most consequential layers of American law remains largely absent from existing machine-readable corpora: local ordinances. Local codes govern zoning, housing, business licensing, public health, noise, animal control, and many other domains of everyday regulation, but they are fragmented across vendor platforms designed for human browsing rather than bulk research access. We introduce LOCUS - the Local Ordinance Corpus for the United States - a comprehensive corpus and county-harmonized access layer for U.S. municipal and county ordinance codes. The raw corpus, available for release to researchers, represents nearly all publicly available municipal and county ordinance codes. The resulting raw corpus contains codes from 9,239 cities and counties. A smaller county-harmonized LOCUS access layer provides coverage for the largest 2,309 of 3,144 U.S. counties, accounting for a majority of the population. We use OCR to handle the myriad of document formats that have kept the law from being a public resource. We release the corpus with coverage metadata to support reproducibility, downstream legal AI research, and the incremental expansion of machine-readable access to local law. We train a collection of ModernBERT-based classifiers and scorers to facilitate analyzing U.S. local law among several dimensions, such as opacity and paternalism, that have not previously been studied at this scale. LOCUS-v1 and its derivative models are available at: https://huggingface.co/datasets/LocalLaws/LOCUS-v1

### [141] [Learning User Simulators with Turing Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19336)
*Yingshan Susan Wang,Cedegao E. Zhang,Linlu Qiu,Zexue He,Pengyuan Li,Alex Pentland,Roger P. Levy,Yoon Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Turing-RL方法，通过基于图灵测试的强化学习训练用户模拟器，使LLM生成与真实用户难以区分的回复，在对话和论坛讨论两个领域均优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有用户模拟方法通常训练LLM匹配单一真实回复（通过最大似然或相似度奖励），但这种方式难以生成与真实用户无差别的交互行为。作者希望探索更有效的训练范式。

Method: 提出Turing-RL框架，使用判别式图灵奖励，以LLM作为裁判评估生成回复与真实用户回复的不可区分性，用户模拟器LLM通过强化学习优化该奖励。

Result: 在对话聊天和Reddit论坛讨论两个领域，Turing-RL在LLM评估和人工评估指标上均一致优于基线方法。

Conclusion: 优化回复的不可区分性（而非匹配单一真实回复）是训练用户模拟器的有效策略。

Abstract: Learning to simulate human users in interactive settings could advance the training of agent assistants, evaluation of personalization systems, research in the social sciences, and more. Existing approaches generally do so by training a large language model (LLM) to match a single ground truth response, either by maximizing the log probability or by using a similarity reward. We instead propose {Turing-RL}: a Turing-Test-based reinforcement learning approach for training user simulator models. {Turing-RL} uses a discriminative Turing reward with an LLM judge to score how indistinguishable a generated response is from the real user's given the user's history, and the user simulator LLM learns to produce responses indistinguishable from what the user could have said with such rewards. Across two different domains--conversational chat and Reddit forum discussion--we find that {Turing-RL} consistently outperforms baseline methods on both LLM and human evaluation metrics. Our study suggests that optimizing for indistinguishability, rather than response matching, is effective for learning user simulators.

</details>
